<script type="text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function() {

    (function(exports) {
        // 滚动图
        var SF = new ScrollPic();
        SF.scrollContId = "J_Scroll_A_List";
        SF.arrLeftId = "J_Scroll_A_Prev";
        SF.arrRightId = "J_Scroll_A_Next";
        SF.dotListId = "J_Scroll_A_Dots";
        SF.dotClassName = "";
        SF.dotOnClassName = "current";
        SF.listType = "";
        SF.listEvent = "onmouseover";
        SF.frameWidth = 350;
        SF.pageWidth = 350;
        SF.upright = false;
        SF.speed = 20;
        SF.space = 50;
        SF.autoPlay = true;
        SF.autoPlayTime = 5;
        SF.circularly = true;
        SF.initialize();
        exports.FocusSlide = SF;
        // 播放器设置
        exports.sinaBokePlayerConfig_o = {
            container: "flashPlayer",
            width: 350,
            height: 260,
            playerWidth: 350,
            playerHeight: 260,
            autoLoad: 1,
            autoPlay: 1,
            as: 0,
            pid: 6,
            tjAD: 0,
            tj: 0,
            continuePlayer: 1,
            casualPlay: 1,
            head: 0,
            logo: 0,
            share: 0,
            thumbUrl: ""
        };
    })(window);

    (function(exports) {
        var Util = {
            byId: function(id) {
                return document.getElementById(id)
            },
            byClass: function(str, root, tag) {
                if (root) {
                    root = typeof root == "string" ? document.getElementById(root) : root
                } else {
                    root = document.body
                }
                tag = tag || "*";
                var els = root.getElementsByTagName(tag),
                    arr = [];
                for (var i = 0, n = els.length; i < n; i++) {
                    for (var j = 0, k = els[i].className.split(" "), l = k.length; j < l; j++) {
                        if (k[j] == str) {
                            arr.push(els[i]);
                            break
                        }
                    }
                }
                return arr
            },
            bindEvent: function(o, s, fn) {
                if (o.attachEvent) {
                    o.attachEvent('on' + s, fn)
                } else {
                    o.addEventListener(s, fn, false)
                }
                return o
            },
            extend: function(target, source, deep) {
                target = target || {};
                var sType = typeof source,
                    i = 0,
                    options;
                if (sType === 'undefined' || sType === 'boolean') {
                    deep = sType === 'boolean' ? source : false;
                    source = target;
                    target = this
                }
                if (typeof source !== 'object' && Object.prototype.toString.call(source) !== '[object Function]') {
                    source = {}
                }
                while (i <= 2) {
                    options = i === 1 ? target : source;
                    if (options !== null) {
                        for (var name in options) {
                            var src = target[name],
                                copy = options[name];
                            if (target === copy) {
                                continue
                            }
                            if (deep && copy && typeof copy === 'object' && !copy.nodeType) {
                                target[name] = this.extend(src || (copy.length !== null ? [] : {}), copy, deep)
                            } else if (copy !== undefined) {
                                target[name] = copy
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    i++
                }
                return target
            }
        };
        var Player = function(id, options) {
            var self = this;
            self.wrapId = id;
            self.inited = false;
            self.options = self._setOptions(options);
            self.dom = self._getDom(id);
            self.init();
        };
        Player.prototype = {
            init: function() {
                var self = this;
                var opt = self.options;
                var data = self.data = [];
                self.index = 0;
                self.fold = true;
                var triggers = self.dom.triggers;
                var tLength = triggers.length / 2;
                for (var i = 0; i < tLength; i++) {
                    var cItem = triggers[i];
                    var info = cItem.getAttribute('play-data').split('-');
                    var url = cItem.getAttribute('url-data');
                    var title = cItem.getAttribute('title-data');
                    if (info) {
                        data.push({
                            vid: info[0],
                            pid: info[1],
                            vAds: info[2],
                            url: url,
                            title: title,
                            itself: cItem
                        })
                    }
                };
                self._bindEvents();
                self.inited = true
            },
            _setOptions: function(options) {
                var defaults = this.defaults = {
                    playerClass: 'J_Focus_Player',
                    triggerClass: 'J_Focus_Trigger',
                    closeClass: 'J_Focus_Close'
                };
                return Util.extend(defaults, options, true)
            },
            _getDom: function(id) {
                var self = this;
                var opt = self.options;
                var dom = {
                    wrap: Util.byId(id),
                    player: Util.byClass(opt.playerClass, this.wrap, 'div')[0],
                    triggers: Util.byClass(opt.triggerClass, this.wrap, 'a'),
                    close: Util.byClass(opt.closeClass, this.wrap, 'a')[0]
                };
                return dom;
            },
            _createPlayer: function() {
                SinaBokePlayer_o.addVars('HTML5Player_controlBar', true);
                SinaBokePlayer_o.addVars('HTML5Player_autoChangeBGColor', false);
                SinaBokePlayer_o.showFlashPlayer()
            },
            stop: function() {
                Util.byId('flashPlayer').innerHTML = '';
            },
            play: function() {
                var self = this;
                var cData = self.data[self.index];
                Util.byId("myMovie").playVideo(cData.vid, cData.pid, cData.vAds);
                self.firstPlay = false;
            },
            _unfold: function(num) {
                var self = this;
                self.fold = false;
                self.index = num;
                self.dom.player.style.display = 'block';
                Util.byId('flashPlayer').innerHTML = '';
                self._createPlayer();
                FocusSlide&&(FocusSlide.autoPlay = false);
            },
            _fold: function() {
                var self = this;
                self.stop();
                self.dom.player.style.display = 'none';
                self.fold = true;
                FocusSlide&&(FocusSlide.autoPlay = true);
            },
            _bindEvents: function() {
                var self = this;
                var triggers = self.dom.triggers;
                var close = self.dom.close;
                var tLength = triggers.length;
                var trueNum = tLength / 2;
                for (var i = 0; i < tLength; i++) {
                    (function(i) {
                        var t = triggers[i];
                        Util.bindEvent(t, 'click', function() {
                            self._unfold(i % trueNum);
                            return false
                        })
                    })(i);
                };
                Util.bindEvent(close, 'click', function() {
                    self._fold();
                    return false;
                })
            }
        };
        exports.CommonUtil = Util;
        exports.FocusPlayer = Player;
    })(window);
    (function(exports){
        // 初始化
        var FP = new FocusPlayer('J_Focus_Player_Wrap', {
            triggerClass: 'J_Focus_Trigger',
            closeClass: 'J_Focus_Close'
        });
        exports.playCompleted = function() {
            FP.play();
        };
        exports.flashInitCompleted = function() {
            exports.playCompleted();
        };
    })(window);

    });

            $("#J_ruleSpecWrap").slideToggle("slow");
        }
    })

    //tab切换
    function cur(ele,currentClass,tag){
      var ele= $(ele) || ele;
      var tag= tag || "";
      var mark= currentClass || "active";
      ele.addClass(mark).siblings(tag).removeClass(mark);
      }

    function tab(id_tab,tag_tab,id_con,act,fn){
        var act=act || "click";
        var timer;
        var time=0;
        if(act=="mouseover"){
            time=200;
        }       
        $(id_tab).find(tag_tab).bind(act,function(){
                var idx=$(this).index();
                var _this =this;
                timer = setTimeout(function(){
                    cur(_this,"active");

    function search_submit(formname)
    {
        //formname.title.value=0;
        if ((ask_form.title.value == '')||(ask_form.title.value == '请输入您的问题...'))   

        {
                  alert("请输入您的搜索内容");
                  ask_form.title.value="";
                    return false;

        }
        formname.key.value = formname.title.value;
        formname.action="//iask.finance.sina.com.cn/search_engine/search_knowledge_engine.php";
        formname.submit();
        formname.action="//iask.finance.sina.com.cn/question/ask_new_2.php";
    }

    var url = $("#"+game+"_select_id").val();
    if(url==''){
        alert("请选择期数!");
        return false;
    }
    window.open(url); 
};

                        //垂直滚动
                        belle.circularly= true;
        
                        belle.speed = 10;

                        belle.space = 10;
                        //每次移动像素(单位px，越大越快)
                        belle.autoPlay = true;
                        //自动播放
                        belle.autoPlayTime = 5;
                        //自动播放间隔时间(秒)
                        belle.initialize();
                    
                </script>
